<script type="text/javascript">
    (function () {

        var urlBuilder = new Skyscanner.Common.UrlBuilder(null, { version: Skyscanner.scaffoldversion });
        var src = urlBuilder.buildStaticResourceUrl('scripts/translations/g/cookiepolicy.' + (Skyscanner.ComponentContext['locale'] || 'en-GB') + '.js');

        var onTranslationsLoaded = function() {
            var template = $('#cookie-policy-template').html();
            var translator = new Skyscanner.Common.Translate();
            var translations = {
                ktxtCookiePolicyHeaderBar: translator.translate('ktxtCookiePolicyHeaderBar'),
                ktxtCookiePolicyHeaderBarOk: (translator.translate('ktxtCookiePolicyHeaderBarOk') || '').toUpperCase()
            };
            var html = _.template(template)(translations).replace('@@link@@', '/cookiepolicy.aspx');
            $('body').prepend(html);
            var trackingEvent = {
                mixpanel: [{ name: 'Cookie Policy Alert Visible' }]
            }
            Skyscanner.Common.observer.publish('tracking-event', trackingEvent);
            Skyscanner.Common.observer.publish('cookie-policy-opened');
            Skyscanner.Api.localStorage.init('web').trySetValue('user.cookiePolicyShown', true, true);

            $('#cookie a.acknowledge').click(function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                Skyscanner.Api.localStorage.init('web').trySetValue('user.cookiePolicyAcknowledged', true, true);
                $('#cookie').hide();
                Skyscanner.Common.observer.publish('cookie-policy-closed');
                return false;
            });    
        };
        $.ajax({
            url: src,
            success: onTranslationsLoaded,
            dataType: "script",
            cache: true
        });
    })();        
</script>
